     1	/**
     2	 * Domain Coverage Query
     3	 *
     4	 * Returns a value-pair coverage matrix for a domain: how many completed
     5	 * trial batches (runs) exist for each Schwartz value pair vignette.
     6	 * Scoped to the same 10-value set used in domain analysis.
     7	 */
     8	
     9	import { builder } from '../builder.js';
    10	import { db, resolveDefinitionContent } from '@valuerank/db';
    11	
    12	import {
    13	  COVERAGE_VALUE_KEYS,
    14	  type CoverageValueKey,
    15	  extractValuePair,
    16	  getCoverageBatchGroupId,
    17	  getCoverageBatchIncrement,
    18	  selectPrimaryDefinitionCounts,
    19	  computePerModelTrialCounts,
    20	  deduplicateRunsByGroupId,
    21	} from './domain-coverage-utils.js';
    22	import { resolveEffectiveDefaultModelIds } from './domain/shared.js';
    23	import {
    24	  DomainValueCoverageResultRef,
    25	  type DomainValueCoverageCell,
    26	  type CoverageModelOption,
    27	  runMatchesSignature,
    28	} from './domain-coverage-gql-types.js';
    29	
    30	const VALUE_PAIR_RESOLVE_CHUNK_SIZE = 20;
    31	
    32	builder.queryField('domainValueCoverage', (t) =>
    33	  t.field({
    34	    type: DomainValueCoverageResultRef,
    35	    nullable: true,
    36	    description: `
    37	      Returns a Schwartz value-pair coverage matrix for a domain.
    38	
    39	      Each cell shows how many completed trial batches (runs) exist for the vignette
    40	      that tests that pair of values in conflict. Optionally filtered to count only
    41	      runs that included the specified model IDs.
    42	
    43	      The matrix is symmetric: each unique value pair appears once, with the cell key
    44	      sorted alphabetically (valueA < valueB). Diagonal cells are omitted.
    45	    `,
    46	    args: {
    47	      domainId: t.arg.id({
    48	        required: true,
    49	        description: 'Domain to compute coverage for',
    50	      }),
    51	      modelIds: t.arg.stringList({
    52	        required: false,
    53	        description: 'If provided, only count runs that included at least one of these model IDs',
    54	      }),
    55	      signature: t.arg.string({
    56	        required: false,
    57	        description: 'If provided, only count completed runs matching this trial signature',
    58	      }),
    59	    },
    60	    resolve: async (_root, args, ctx) => {
    61	      const domainId = String(args.domainId);
    62	      const filterModelIds = args.modelIds?.map(String) ?? [];
    63	      const selectedSignature = typeof args.signature === 'string' && args.signature.trim() !== ''
    64	        ? args.signature.trim()
    65	        : null;
    66	
    67	      ctx.log.debug({ domainId, filterModelIds, selectedSignature }, 'Computing domain value coverage');
    68	
    69	      const domain = await db.domain.findUnique({ where: { id: domainId }, select: { id: true, defaultModelIds: true } });
    70	      if (!domain) return null;
    71	
    72	      // Resolve effective model IDs: use domain-specific list if set, otherwise fall back
    73	      // to globally defaulted models (isDefault=true, ACTIVE) from the Models settings page.
    74	      const effectiveModelIds = await resolveEffectiveDefaultModelIds(domain.defaultModelIds);
    75	
    76	      // Pre-fetch labels for effective models so we can populate model breakdown
    77	      const defaultModelLabelById = new Map<string, string>();
    78	      if (effectiveModelIds.length > 0) {
    79	        const defaultModelRows = await db.llmModel.findMany({
    80	          where: { modelId: { in: effectiveModelIds } },
    81	          select: { modelId: true, displayName: true },
    82	        });
    83	        for (const row of defaultModelRows) {
    84	          defaultModelLabelById.set(row.modelId, row.displayName);
    85	        }
    86	      }
    87	
    88	      // Fetch all non-deleted definitions (need IDs to resolve content)
    89	      const definitions = await db.definition.findMany({
    90	        where: { domainId, deletedAt: null },
    91	        select: { id: true, name: true },
    92	        orderBy: { createdAt: 'asc' },
    93	      });
    94	
    95	      // Map definition ID -> value pair (only those with recognized canonical pair)
    96	      type DefValuePair = { valueA: CoverageValueKey; valueB: CoverageValueKey; name: string };
    97	      const pairByDefinitionId = new Map<string, DefValuePair>();
    98	      // Map directional pair key -> definition IDs (to detect multi-vignette cells)
    99	      const definitionsByPairKey = new Map<string, string[]>();
   100	
   101	      // Resolve definition contents in chunks to handle inheritance
   102	      for (let offset = 0; offset < definitions.length; offset += VALUE_PAIR_RESOLVE_CHUNK_SIZE) {
   103	        const batch = definitions.slice(offset, offset + VALUE_PAIR_RESOLVE_CHUNK_SIZE);
   104	        const settled = await Promise.allSettled(
   105	          batch.map(async (def) => {
   106	            const resolvedContent = (await resolveDefinitionContent(def.id) as { resolvedContent: unknown }).resolvedContent;
   107	            const pair = extractValuePair(resolvedContent);
   108	            if (pair == null) return;
   109	
   110	            pairByDefinitionId.set(def.id, { ...pair, name: def.name ?? '' });
   111	            const key = `${pair.valueA}::${pair.valueB}`;
   112	            const existing = definitionsByPairKey.get(key) ?? [];
   113	            existing.push(def.id);
   114	            definitionsByPairKey.set(key, existing);
   115	          })
   116	        );
   117	        settled.forEach((result, idx) => {
   118	          if (result.status === 'rejected') {
   119	            ctx.log.error(
   120	              { err: result.reason as unknown, definitionId: batch[idx]?.id },
   121	              'Failed to resolve definition content for coverage grid'
   122	            );
   123	          }
   124	        });
   125	      }
   126	
   127	      // Count completed runs per definition, optionally filtered by signature and model
   128	      const definitionIds = Array.from(pairByDefinitionId.keys());
   129	      const batchCountByDefinitionId = new Map<string, number>();
   130	      const pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId = new Map<string, number>();
   131	      const pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
   132	      const pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId = new Map<string, Map<string, number>>();
   133	      const latestMatchingRunIdByDefinitionId = new Map<string, string>();
   134	      const latestAggregateRunIdByDefinitionId = new Map<string, string>();
   135	      const incompleteBatchCountByDefinitionId = new Map<string, number>();
   136	      const signatureScopedRunsByDefinitionId = new Map<string, Array<{
   137	        id: string;
   138	        definitionId: string;
   139	        config: unknown;
   140	        transcripts: Array<{ modelId: string }>;
   141	      }>>();
   142	      // Non-aggregate runs per definition (for per-model trial count computation)
   143	      const nonAggregateRunsByDefinitionId = new Map<string, Array<{
   144	        config: unknown;
   145	        transcripts: Array<{ modelId: string }>;
   146	      }>>();
   147	
   148	      if (definitionIds.length > 0) {
   149	        const completedRuns = await db.run.findMany({
   150	          where: {
   151	            definitionId: { in: definitionIds },
   152	            status: 'COMPLETED',
   153	            deletedAt: null,
   154	          },
   155	          orderBy: [{ definitionId: 'asc' }, { createdAt: 'desc' }],
   156	          select: {
   157	            id: true,
   158	            definitionId: true,
   159	            config: true,
   160	            transcripts: {
   161	              where: { deletedAt: null },
   162	              select: { modelId: true },
   163	            },
   164	            _count: {
   165	              select: { scenarioSelections: true },
   166	            },
   167	          },
   168	        });
   169	
   170	        const signatureScopedRuns = selectedSignature === null
   171	          ? completedRuns
   172	          : completedRuns.filter((run) => runMatchesSignature(run.config, selectedSignature));
   173	
   174	        for (const run of signatureScopedRuns) {
   175	          const existingRuns = signatureScopedRunsByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? [];
   176	          existingRuns.push(run);
   177	          signatureScopedRunsByDefinitionId.set(run.definitionId, existingRuns);
   178	
   179	          const isAggregateRun = (run.config as { isAggregate?: boolean } | null)?.isAggregate === true;
   180	          if (isAggregateRun) {
   181	            if (!latestAggregateRunIdByDefinitionId.has(run.definitionId)) {
   182	              latestAggregateRunIdByDefinitionId.set(run.definitionId, run.id);
   183	            }
   184	            continue;
   185	          }
   186	
   187	          // Completeness check: flag if actual transcript count < expected.
   188	          // Expected = scenarioSelections × models.length × samplesPerScenario.
   189	          const samplesPerScenario =
   190	            (run.config as { samplesPerScenario?: unknown } | null)?.samplesPerScenario;
   191	          const configModels = (run.config as { models?: unknown } | null)?.models;
   192	          const modelCount = Array.isArray(configModels) ? configModels.length : 0;
   193	          const expectedCount =
   194	            run._count.scenarioSelections * modelCount * getCoverageBatchIncrement(samplesPerScenario);
   195	          if (modelCount > 0 && run.transcripts.length < expectedCount) {
   196	            incompleteBatchCountByDefinitionId.set(
   197	              run.definitionId,
   198	              (incompleteBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? 0) + 1,
   199	            );
   200	          }
   201	
   202	          // Track non-aggregate runs for per-model trial count computation
   203	          if (effectiveModelIds.length > 0) {
   204	            const nonAggregateRuns = nonAggregateRunsByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? [];
   205	            nonAggregateRuns.push({ config: run.config, transcripts: run.transcripts });
   206	            nonAggregateRunsByDefinitionId.set(run.definitionId, nonAggregateRuns);
   207	          }
   208	
   209	          const matchesModelFilter = filterModelIds.length === 0
   210	            || run.transcripts.some((transcript) => filterModelIds.includes(transcript.modelId));
   211	          if (!matchesModelFilter) continue;
   212	
   213	          if (!latestMatchingRunIdByDefinitionId.has(run.definitionId)) {
   214	            latestMatchingRunIdByDefinitionId.set(run.definitionId, run.id);
   215	          }
   216	          const increment = getCoverageBatchIncrement(samplesPerScenario);
   217	          batchCountByDefinitionId.set(
   218	            run.definitionId,
   219	            (batchCountByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? 0) + increment,
   220	          );
   221	
   222	          const pairedBatchGroupId = getCoverageBatchGroupId(run.config);
   223	
   224	          if (pairedBatchGroupId === null) {
   225	            pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.set(
   226	              run.definitionId,
   227	              (pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? 0) + increment,
   228	            );
   229	            continue;
   230	          }
   231	
   232	          const seenGroupIds = pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? new Set<string>();
   233	          if (!seenGroupIds.has(pairedBatchGroupId)) {
   234	            seenGroupIds.add(pairedBatchGroupId);
   235	            pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId.set(run.definitionId, seenGroupIds);
   236	            pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.set(
   237	              run.definitionId,
   238	              (pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(run.definitionId) ?? 0) + increment,
   239	            );
   240	            // Track increment per group ID for cross-definition dedup
   241	            const defIncrements = pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId.get(run.definitionId) ?? new Map<string, number>();
   242	            defIncrements.set(pairedBatchGroupId, increment);
   243	            pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId.set(run.definitionId, defIncrements);
   244	          }
   245	        }
   246	      }
   247	
   248	      const availableModelIds = new Set<string>();
   249	      for (const runs of signatureScopedRunsByDefinitionId.values()) {
   250	        for (const run of runs) {
   251	          for (const transcript of run.transcripts) {
   252	            availableModelIds.add(transcript.modelId);
   253	          }
   254	        }
   255	      }
   256	
   257	      const modelDetailRows =
   258	        availableModelIds.size > 0
   259	          ? await db.llmModel.findMany({
   260	            where: { modelId: { in: Array.from(availableModelIds) } },
   261	            select: { modelId: true, displayName: true },
   262	            orderBy: { displayName: 'asc' },
   263	          })
   264	          : [];
   265	
   266	      const availableModels: CoverageModelOption[] = modelDetailRows.map((m) => ({
   267	        modelId: m.modelId,
   268	        label: m.displayName,
   269	      }));
   270	
   271	      // Build the symmetric 45-cell matrix (one cell per unique sorted pair)
   272	      const values = [...COVERAGE_VALUE_KEYS] as string[];
   273	      const cells: DomainValueCoverageCell[] = [];
   274	
   275	      for (const valueA of COVERAGE_VALUE_KEYS) {
   276	        for (const valueB of COVERAGE_VALUE_KEYS) {
   277	          // Only emit sorted pairs: skip diagonal and reversed pairs
   278	          if (valueA.localeCompare(valueB) >= 0) continue;
   279	
   280	          const key = `${valueA}::${valueB}`;
   281	          const defIdsForPair = definitionsByPairKey.get(key) ?? [];
   282	
   283	          if (defIdsForPair.length === 0) {
   284	            cells.push({
   285	              valueA,
   286	              valueB,
   287	              batchCount: 0,
   288	              pairedBatchCount: 0,
   289	              incompleteBatchCount: 0,
   290	              definitionId: null,
   291	              definitionName: null,
   292	              aggregateRunId: null,
   293	              minTrialCount: null,
   294	              maxTrialCount: null,
   295	              modelBreakdown: null,
   296	            });
   297	          } else {
   298	            // Use the total counts across all definitions for the visible cell, but
   299	            // still choose one stable definition for the analysis link target.
   300	            const { primaryDefinitionId, batchCount, pairedBatchCount } = selectPrimaryDefinitionCounts(
   301	              defIdsForPair,
   302	              batchCountByDefinitionId,
   303	              pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId,
   304	              pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId,
   305	              pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId,
   306	            );
   307	            const primaryDefId = primaryDefinitionId ?? '';
   308	            const primaryPair = pairByDefinitionId.get(primaryDefId);
   309	            const aggregateRunId = primaryDefId === ''
   310	              ? null
   311	              : (latestAggregateRunIdByDefinitionId.get(primaryDefId)
   312	                ?? latestMatchingRunIdByDefinitionId.get(primaryDefId)
   313	                ?? null);
   314	
   315	            // Sum incompleteBatchCount across all definitions for this pair
   316	            const incompleteBatchCount = defIdsForPair.reduce(
   317	              (sum, defId) => sum + (incompleteBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0),
   318	              0,
   319	            );
   320	
   321	            // Compute per-model trial counts across all definitions for this pair.
   322	            // Deduplicate by group ID first: A-first and B-first companion definitions
   323	            // share the same jobChoiceBatchGroupId, so flatMapping across both would
   324	            // double-count each paired batch.
   325	            const allNonAggregateRunsForPair = deduplicateRunsByGroupId(
   326	              defIdsForPair.flatMap((defId) => nonAggregateRunsByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? []),
   327	            );
   328	            const { minTrialCount, maxTrialCount, modelBreakdown } = computePerModelTrialCounts(
   329	              allNonAggregateRunsForPair,
   330	              effectiveModelIds,
   331	              defaultModelLabelById,
   332	            );
   333	
   334	            cells.push({
   335	              valueA,
   336	              valueB,
   337	              batchCount,
   338	              pairedBatchCount,
   339	              incompleteBatchCount,
   340	              definitionId: primaryDefId !== '' ? primaryDefId : null,
   341	              definitionName: primaryPair?.name ?? null,
   342	              aggregateRunId,
   343	              minTrialCount,
   344	              maxTrialCount,
   345	              modelBreakdown,
   346	            });
   347	          }
   348	        }
   349	      }
   350	
   351	      ctx.log.debug({ domainId, cellCount: cells.length }, 'Domain value coverage computed');
   352	      return { domainId, values, cells, availableModels };
   353	    },
   354	  })
   355	);

     1	import { DOMAIN_ANALYSIS_VALUE_KEYS, extractValuePair, toPascalCaseKey, type DomainAnalysisValueKey } from './domain-analysis-values.js';
     2	
     3	export const COVERAGE_VALUE_KEYS = DOMAIN_ANALYSIS_VALUE_KEYS;
     4	export type CoverageValueKey = DomainAnalysisValueKey;
     5	export { extractValuePair, toPascalCaseKey };
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Extract the two canonical value dimension names from a definition's resolved content JSON.
     9	 * Returns null if the definition does not have exactly two recognized value dimensions.
    10	 */
    11	export function selectPrimaryDefinitionCount(
    12	  definitionIds: readonly string[],
    13	  batchCountByDefinitionId: ReadonlyMap<string, number>,
    14	): { primaryDefinitionId: string | null; batchCount: number } {
    15	  const uniqueDefinitionIds = Array.from(new Set(definitionIds));
    16	  if (uniqueDefinitionIds.length === 0) {
    17	    return { primaryDefinitionId: null, batchCount: 0 };
    18	  }
    19	
    20	  const primaryDefinitionId = uniqueDefinitionIds.reduce((best, defId) => {
    21	    const bestCount = batchCountByDefinitionId.get(best) ?? 0;
    22	    const thisCount = batchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0;
    23	    return thisCount > bestCount ? defId : best;
    24	  }, uniqueDefinitionIds[0] ?? '');
    25	
    26	  return {
    27	    primaryDefinitionId: primaryDefinitionId === '' ? null : primaryDefinitionId,
    28	    batchCount: primaryDefinitionId === '' ? 0 : (batchCountByDefinitionId.get(primaryDefinitionId) ?? 0),
    29	  };
    30	}
    31	
    32	export function selectPrimaryDefinitionCounts(
    33	  definitionIds: readonly string[],
    34	  batchCountByDefinitionId: ReadonlyMap<string, number>,
    35	  pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId: ReadonlyMap<string, number>,
    36	  pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId?: ReadonlyMap<string, ReadonlySet<string>>,
    37	  pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId?: ReadonlyMap<string, ReadonlyMap<string, number>>,
    38	): { primaryDefinitionId: string | null; batchCount: number; pairedBatchCount: number } {
    39	  const uniqueDefinitionIds = Array.from(new Set(definitionIds));
    40	  if (uniqueDefinitionIds.length === 0) {
    41	    return { primaryDefinitionId: null, batchCount: 0, pairedBatchCount: 0 };
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  const primaryDefinitionId = uniqueDefinitionIds.reduce((best, defId) => {
    45	    const bestBatchCount = batchCountByDefinitionId.get(best) ?? 0;
    46	    const thisBatchCount = batchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0;
    47	    if (thisBatchCount > bestBatchCount) {
    48	      return defId;
    49	    }
    50	    if (thisBatchCount < bestBatchCount) {
    51	      return best;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    const bestPairedCount = pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(best) ?? 0;
    55	    const thisPairedCount = pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0;
    56	    if (thisPairedCount > bestPairedCount) {
    57	      return defId;
    58	    }
    59	    if (thisPairedCount < bestPairedCount) {
    60	      return best;
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    return defId.localeCompare(best) < 0 ? defId : best;
    64	  }, uniqueDefinitionIds[0] ?? '');
    65	
    66	  const batchCount = uniqueDefinitionIds.reduce(
    67	    (total, defId) => total + (batchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0),
    68	    0,
    69	  );
    70	
    71	  // Deduplicate paired batch counts across companion definitions.
    72	  // A_first and B_first share the same group IDs, so we merge group→increment
    73	  // maps and take the max increment per group (not sum). Ungrouped runs are summed.
    74	  let pairedBatchCount: number;
    75	  if (pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId != null && pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId != null) {
    76	    // Merge increments: for each group ID, take the max increment across definitions
    77	    // (companions have the same sps, so max === any, but max is safer)
    78	    const mergedIncrements = new Map<string, number>();
    79	    let ungroupedTotal = 0;
    80	    for (const defId of uniqueDefinitionIds) {
    81	      const defIncrements = pairedBatchIncrementsByGroupId.get(defId);
    82	      if (defIncrements != null) {
    83	        for (const [gid, inc] of defIncrements) {
    84	          mergedIncrements.set(gid, Math.max(mergedIncrements.get(gid) ?? 0, inc));
    85	        }
    86	      }
    87	      // Ungrouped portion: pairedBatchCount minus grouped total for this definition
    88	      const defPairedCount = pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0;
    89	      const defGroupedTotal = defIncrements != null
    90	        ? Array.from(defIncrements.values()).reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0)
    91	        : 0;
    92	      ungroupedTotal += Math.max(0, defPairedCount - defGroupedTotal);
    93	    }
    94	    pairedBatchCount = Array.from(mergedIncrements.values()).reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0) + ungroupedTotal;
    95	  } else if (pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId != null) {
    96	    // Legacy path: group IDs available but no increment tracking — count unique groups
    97	    const mergedGroupIds = new Set<string>();
    98	    let ungroupedCount = 0;
    99	    for (const defId of uniqueDefinitionIds) {
   100	      const groupIds = pairedBatchGroupIdsByDefinitionId.get(defId);
   101	      if (groupIds != null) {
   102	        for (const gid of groupIds) {
   103	          mergedGroupIds.add(gid);
   104	        }
   105	      }
   106	      const defPairedCount = pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0;
   107	      const defGroupedCount = groupIds?.size ?? 0;
   108	      ungroupedCount += Math.max(0, defPairedCount - defGroupedCount);
   109	    }
   110	    pairedBatchCount = mergedGroupIds.size + ungroupedCount;
   111	  } else {
   112	    // Fallback: sum per-definition counts
   113	    pairedBatchCount = uniqueDefinitionIds.reduce(
   114	      (total, defId) => total + (pairedBatchCountByDefinitionId.get(defId) ?? 0),
   115	      0,
   116	    );
   117	  }
   118	
   119	  return {
   120	    primaryDefinitionId: primaryDefinitionId === '' ? null : primaryDefinitionId,
   121	    batchCount,
   122	    pairedBatchCount,
   123	  };
   124	}
   125	
   126	export function getCoverageBatchIncrement(samplesPerScenario: unknown): number {
   127	  return Number.isInteger(samplesPerScenario) && (samplesPerScenario as number) >= 1
   128	    ? (samplesPerScenario as number)
   129	    : 1;
   130	}
   131	
   132	export type CoverageModelBreakdown = { modelId: string; label: string; trialCount: number };
   133	
   134	/**
   135	 * Deduplicate a list of runs by their paired-batch group ID.
   136	 *
   137	 * A-first and B-first companion definitions for the same value pair share the
   138	 * same `jobChoiceBatchGroupId` / `pairedBatchGroupId`. When runs are collected
   139	 * across both companion definitions and flattened into a single list, each paired
   140	 * batch appears twice. Call this before any aggregation (trial counts, model
   141	 * breakdowns, etc.) to ensure each batch is counted exactly once.
   142	 *
   143	 * Runs without a group ID (ungrouped / unpaired) are always kept.
   144	 */
   145	export function deduplicateRunsByGroupId<T extends { config: unknown }>(runs: ReadonlyArray<T>): T[] {
   146	  const seenGroupIds = new Set<string>();
   147	  return runs.filter((run) => {
   148	    const groupId = getCoverageBatchGroupId(run.config);
   149	    if (groupId === null) return true;
   150	    if (seenGroupIds.has(groupId)) return false;
   151	    seenGroupIds.add(groupId);
   152	    return true;
   153	  });
   154	}
   155	
   156	export function computePerModelTrialCounts(
   157	  runs: ReadonlyArray<{ config: unknown; transcripts: ReadonlyArray<{ modelId: string }> }>,
   158	  defaultModelIds: readonly string[],
   159	  modelLabelById: ReadonlyMap<string, string>,
   160	): { minTrialCount: number | null; maxTrialCount: number | null; modelBreakdown: CoverageModelBreakdown[] | null } {
   161	  if (defaultModelIds.length === 0) {
   162	    return { minTrialCount: null, maxTrialCount: null, modelBreakdown: null };
   163	  }
   164	
   165	  // Caller is responsible for deduplicating paired runs before passing them here.
   166	  // Use deduplicateRunsByGroupId() at the call site when collecting runs across
   167	  // companion definitions for the same value pair.
   168	  const trialCountByModel = new Map<string, number>(
   169	    defaultModelIds.map((modelId) => [modelId, 0]),
   170	  );
   171	
   172	  for (const run of runs) {
   173	    const increment = getCoverageBatchIncrement(
   174	      (run.config as { samplesPerScenario?: unknown } | null)?.samplesPerScenario,
   175	    );
   176	    const transcriptModelIds = new Set(run.transcripts.map((t) => t.modelId));
   177	    for (const modelId of defaultModelIds) {
   178	      if (transcriptModelIds.has(modelId)) {
   179	        trialCountByModel.set(modelId, (trialCountByModel.get(modelId) ?? 0) + increment);
   180	      }
   181	    }
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  const modelBreakdown: CoverageModelBreakdown[] = defaultModelIds.map((modelId) => ({
   185	    modelId,
   186	    label: modelLabelById.get(modelId) ?? modelId,
   187	    trialCount: trialCountByModel.get(modelId) ?? 0,
   188	  }));
   189	
   190	  const counts = modelBreakdown.map((b) => b.trialCount);
   191	  const minTrialCount = Math.min(...counts);
   192	  const maxTrialCount = Math.max(...counts);
   193	
   194	  return { minTrialCount, maxTrialCount, modelBreakdown };
   195	}
   196	
   197	export function getCoverageBatchGroupId(runConfig: unknown): string | null {
   198	  const config = runConfig as {
   199	    jobChoiceBatchGroupId?: unknown;
   200	    pairedBatchGroupId?: unknown;
   201	  } | null;
   202	
   203	  const raw = typeof config?.jobChoiceBatchGroupId === 'string'
   204	    ? config.jobChoiceBatchGroupId
   205	    : typeof config?.pairedBatchGroupId === 'string'
   206	      ? config.pairedBatchGroupId
   207	      : null;
   208	
   209	  return raw != null && raw.trim().length > 0 ? raw.trim() : null;
   210	}

    19	
    20	/**
    21	 * Check if a run's cost estimate would overdraw any provider's budget.
    22	 * Only providers with a non-null balance are considered.
    23	 */
    24	export function checkBudgetOverdraft(
    25	  costEstimate: CostEstimate | null,
    26	  providers: LlmProvidersQueryResult['llmProviders']
    27	): OverdraftProvider[] {
    28	  if (!costEstimate?.perModel || costEstimate.perModel.length === 0) return [];
    29	
    30	  // Group estimated cost by provider prefix
    31	  const costByProvider = new Map<string, number>();
    32	  for (const item of costEstimate.perModel) {
    33	    const colonIdx = item.modelId.indexOf(':');
    34	    if (colonIdx < 0) continue;
    35	    const providerName = item.modelId.slice(0, colonIdx);
    36	    costByProvider.set(providerName, (costByProvider.get(providerName) ?? 0) + item.totalCost);
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  const overdrafts: OverdraftProvider[] = [];
    40	  for (const provider of providers) {
    41	    if (provider.balance === null) continue;
    42	    const estimatedCost = costByProvider.get(provider.name) ?? 0;
    43	    if (estimatedCost > provider.balance) {
    44	      overdrafts.push({
    45	        name: provider.name,
    46	        displayName: provider.displayName,
    47	        estimatedCost,
    48	        balance: provider.balance,
    49	      });
    50	    }
    51	  }
    52	  return overdrafts;
    53	}

   135	
   136	  const {
   137	    costEstimate: allModelsCostEstimate,
   138	    loading: loadingCost,
   139	    error: costError,
   140	  } = useCostEstimate({
   141	    definitionId,
   142	    models: allAvailableModelIds,
   143	    samplePercentage: isSpecificConditionTrial && scenarioCount
   144	      ? Math.max(1, Math.round((selectedConditionScenarioIds.length / scenarioCount) * 100))
   145	      : formState.samplePercentage,
   146	    samplesPerScenario: formState.samplesPerScenario,
   147	    pause: allAvailableModelIds.length === 0,
   148	  });
   149	
   150	  const costEstimate = allModelsCostEstimate
   151	    ? (() => {
   152	        const selectedPerModel = allModelsCostEstimate.perModel.filter((model) =>
   153	          formState.selectedModels.includes(model.modelId)
   154	        );
   155	        const isUsingFallback = selectedPerModel.some((model) => model.isUsingFallback);
   156	        return {
   157	          ...allModelsCostEstimate,
   158	          total: selectedPerModel.reduce((sum, model) => sum + model.totalCost, 0),
   159	          perModel: selectedPerModel,
   160	          isUsingFallback,
   161	          fallbackReason: isUsingFallback ? allModelsCostEstimate.fallbackReason : null,
   162	        };
   163	      })()
   164	    : null;
   165	
   166	  // Budget-aware form submit handler: intercepts to show warning if overdraft detected
   167	  const handleFormSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) => {
   168	    const providers = providersData?.llmProviders ?? [];
   169	    const overdrafts = checkBudgetOverdraft(costEstimate, providers);
   170	    if (overdrafts.length > 0) {
   171	      e.preventDefault();
   172	      setBudgetOverdrafts(overdrafts);
   173	      return;
   174	    }
   175	    await handleSubmit(e);
   176	  };
   177	
   178	  const handleBudgetProceed = async () => {
   179	    setBudgetOverdrafts([]);
   180	    // Re-submit using the captured form submit callback
   181	    // We trigger handleSubmit with a synthetic event
   182	    const syntheticEvent = { preventDefault: () => {} } as React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>;
   183	    await handleSubmit(syntheticEvent);
   184	  };
   185	
   186	  const totalJobs = estimatedScenarios !== null
   187	    ? estimatedScenarios * formState.selectedModels.length * formState.samplesPerScenario
   188	    : null;
   189	
   190	  return (
   191	    <>
   192	    {budgetOverdrafts.length > 0 && (
   193	      <BudgetWarningDialog
   194	        overdraftProviders={budgetOverdrafts}
   195	        onProceed={() => { void handleBudgetProceed(); }}
   196	        onCancel={() => { setBudgetOverdrafts([]); }}
   197	      />
   198	    )}
   199	    <form onSubmit={handleFormSubmit} className="space-y-6">
   200	      <div>
   201	        <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
   202	          Target Models
   203	        </label>
   204	        {modelsError ? (
   205	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-red-600 p-3 bg-red-50 rounded-lg">
   206	            <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4" />
   207	            <span>Failed to load models: {modelsError.message}</span>
   208	          </div>
   209	        ) : (
   210	          <ModelSelector
   211	            models={models}
   212	            selectedModels={formState.selectedModels}
   213	            onSelectionChange={handleModelSelectionChange}
   214	            loading={loadingModels}
   215	            disabled={isSubmitting}
   216	            costEstimate={costEstimate}
   217	            allModelsCostEstimate={allModelsCostEstimate}
   218	            costLoading={loadingCost}
   219	          />
   220	        )}
   221	        {validationError && (
   222	          <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-red-600">{validationError}</p>
   223	        )}
   224	      </div>
   225	
   226	      {isPairedDefinition && (
   227	        <div className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 p-4 space-y-3">
   228	          <div>
   229	            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">
   230	              Batch Type
   231	            </label>
   232	            <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
   233	              {[
   234	                {
   235	                  value: 'PAIRED_BATCH' as const,
   236	                  title: 'Start Paired Batch',
   237	                  description:
   238	                    'Methodology-safe default. Launches both order variants together.',
   239	                },
   240	                {
   241	                  value: 'AD_HOC_BATCH' as const,
   242	                  title: 'Start Ad Hoc Batch',
   243	                  description:
   244	                    'Exploratory only. Launches just this definition and should be treated as non-methodology-safe by default.',
   245	                },
   246	              ].map((option) => {
   247	                const selected = formState.launchMode === option.value;
   248	                return (
   249	                  // eslint-disable-next-line react/forbid-elements -- Toggle chip requires custom styling
   250	                  <button
   251	                    key={option.value}
   252	                    type="button"
   253	                    onClick={() => handleLaunchModeChange(option.value)}
   254	                    disabled={isSubmitting}
   255	                    className={`rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-left transition-colors ${
   256	                      selected
   257	                        ? 'border-teal-500 bg-teal-50 text-teal-900'
   258	                        : 'border-gray-200 bg-white text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50'
   259	                    } ${isSubmitting ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}`}
   260	                  >
   261	                    <div className="text-sm font-medium">{option.title}</div>
   262	                    <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500">{option.description}</div>
   263	                  </button>
   264	                );
   265	              })}
   266	            </div>
   267	          </div>
   268	        </div>
   269	      )}
   270	
   271	      <div
   272	        data-testid={copyMode === 'paired-batch' ? 'paired-batch-layout' : undefined}
   273	        className={copyMode === 'paired-batch' ? 'grid gap-6 lg:grid-cols-2' : 'space-y-6'}
   274	      >
   275	        <DefinitionPicker
   276	          copyMode={copyMode}
   277	          samplePercentage={formState.samplePercentage}
   278	          estimatedScenarios={estimatedScenarios}
   279	          isSpecificConditionTrial={isSpecificConditionTrial}
   280	          isSubmitting={isSubmitting}
   281	          selectedConditionRowLevel={selectedConditionRowLevel}
   282	          selectedConditionColLevel={selectedConditionColLevel}
   283	          selectedConditionScenarioIds={selectedConditionScenarioIds}
   284	          conditionSelectionTouched={conditionSelectionTouched}
   285	          conditionGrid={conditionGrid}
   286	          loadingConditionGrid={loadingConditionGrid}
   287	          conditionGridError={conditionGridError}
   288	          isConditionModalOpen={isConditionModalOpen}
   289	          modalRowLevel={modalRowLevel}
   290	          modalColLevel={modalColLevel}
   291	          onSampleChange={handleSampleChange}
   292	          onCloseConditionModal={handleCloseConditionModal}
   293	          onImmediateConditionSelect={handleImmediateConditionSelect}
   294	        />
   295	
   296	        <RunConfigPanel
   297	          copyMode={copyMode}
   298	          temperatureInput={formState.temperatureInput}
   299	          samplesPerScenario={formState.samplesPerScenario}
   300	          estimatedScenarios={estimatedScenarios}
   301	          selectedModelCount={formState.selectedModels.length}
   302	          totalJobs={totalJobs}
   303	          isSubmitting={isSubmitting}
   304	          onTemperatureChange={handleTemperatureChange}
   305	          onSamplesPerScenarioChange={handleSamplesPerScenarioChange}
   306	        />
   307	      </div>
   308	
   309	      {formState.selectedModels.length > 0 && (
   310	        <CostBreakdown
   311	          costEstimate={costEstimate}
   312	          loading={loadingCost}
   313	          error={costError}
   314	          compact
   315	        />
   316	      )}
   317	
   318	      <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
   319	        {onCancel && (
   320	          <Button
   321	            type="button"
   322	            variant="secondary"
   323	            onClick={onCancel}
   324	            disabled={isSubmitting}
   325	          >
   326	            Cancel
   327	          </Button>
   328	        )}
   329	        <Button
   330	          type="submit"
   331	          variant="primary"
   332	          disabled={
   333	            isSubmitting ||
   334	            formState.selectedModels.length === 0 ||
   335	            (isSpecificConditionTrial && selectedConditionScenarioIds.length === 0)
   336	          }
   337	        >
   338	          {isSubmitting ? (
   339	            isPairedDefinition
   340	              ? formState.launchMode === 'PAIRED_BATCH'
   341	                ? 'Starting Paired Batch...'
   342	                : 'Starting Ad Hoc Batch...'
   343	              : 'Starting Trial...'
   344	          ) : (
   345	            <>
   346	              <Play className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
   347	              {isPairedDefinition
   348	                ? formState.launchMode === 'PAIRED_BATCH'
   349	                  ? 'Start Paired Batch'
   350	                  : 'Start Ad Hoc Batch'
   351	                : 'Start Trial'}
   352	            </>
   353	          )}
   354	        </Button>
   355	      </div>
   356	    </form>
   357	    </>
   358	  );
   359	}

## Findings
- **HIGH** [CODE-CONFIRMED] The planned `Match Pair Counts` gate is keyed off `aggregateRunId === null`, but the current resolver does not use `aggregateRunId` as an “aggregate-only” flag. It sets that field to `latestAggregateRunId ?? latestMatchingRunId ?? null`, so ordinary covered cells will usually have a non-null value too. That means the action would be hidden on most usable cells, not just aggregate ones. See [`cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L309`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L309) and [`cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L313`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L313).

- **HIGH** [CODE-CONFIRMED] The plan assumes the top-up flow can be layered onto the existing paired-batch form without changing the form API, but the current form state only supports `PAIRED_BATCH | AD_HOC_BATCH`, and `RunForm` hardcodes `defaultLaunchMode: 'PAIRED_BATCH'`. There is no path here to prefill or lock a third launch mode the way the artifact describes. See [`cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L12`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L12), [`cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L41`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L41), [`cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L114`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/useRunForm.ts#L114), and [`cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/RunForm.tsx#L110`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/web/src/components/runs/RunForm.tsx#L110).

- **MEDIUM** [CODE-CONFIRMED] The plan points the shared trial-count helper at `cloud/apps/shared/src/launch-trial-count.ts`, but the repo’s shared workspace is `cloud/packages/shared`, not `cloud/apps/shared`. As written, that path will not match the actual package layout and the import strategy in the artifact will not work without rewriting the location. See [`cloud/packages/shared/package.json#L2`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/packages/shared/package.json#L2).

- **MEDIUM** [CODE-CONFIRMED] The new coverage counts are not scoped to the same `modelIds` filter unless the implementation explicitly preserves the current guard. The existing resolver applies `matchesModelFilter` before incrementing `batchCount` and `pairedBatchCount`; the plan never calls out reusing that filtered run set for the new slot-based counts, so a filtered coverage view could end up with batch counts and condition counts that disagree. See [`cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L209`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L209) through [`cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L229`](file:///Users/chrislaw/valuerank/.claude/worktrees/infallible-bassi-fafa71/cloud/apps/api/src/graphql/queries/domain-coverage.ts#L229).

## Residual Risks
- The artifact still depends on the exact backend slot-accounting rules for `pairedConditionCount` and `orphanedConditionCount`. The provided code does not expose that logic today, so the implementation should be pinned with targeted tests around filtered views, retries, and multi-sample runs before merge.

- The top-up launch path will need a concrete integration point for the new `topUpDirection` field and the locked launch mode. If the implementation keeps `RunForm` as-is, the UI will still be able to submit only the old launch modes.
